2021-04-28 13:12:14.7489| INFO|Program.Main => classLog.LogInfo start 
2021-04-28 13:12:14.7861| INFO|Program.Main => classLog.LogInfo Generowanie danych dla 20210427
2021-04-28 13:12:15.4935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 13:12:15.4935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 13:12:15.4935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-02-28') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-02-28') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

FROM POS.NSYSLOKAL Lokal
join POS.nsysstanowisko s on s.lokalid=Lokal.id
INNER JOIN POS.NSYSKRAJ Kraj on kraj.id = lokal.krajid
WHERE lokal.opis not like ('%Gino%')

order by 1,2

inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-05') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-05') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select

WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa

    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

2021-04-28 13:17:00.4645| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-11') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-11') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-16') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-16') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select

WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa

    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

2021-04-28 13:22:14.4075| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-22') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-22') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-27') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and

WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa

  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

2021-04-28 13:26:50.0470| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-04-02') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-04-02') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-04-07') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-04-07') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

2021-04-28 14:45:03.1580| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-02-28') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-02-28') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-03') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto,

  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid

inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

ELSE tg.terminal

2021-04-28 14:45:33.8237| INFO|Program.Main => Program.SaveOracleToFile => classLog.LogInfo Zapis do katalogu C:\dyskD\wywal\testScan\Stat\statystykaOracle_20210308.csv
2021-04-28 14:45:33.8237| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 14:45:33.8237| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 14:45:33.8237| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-09') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-09') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-14') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto,

  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid

inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

ELSE tg.terminal

  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

2021-04-28 14:46:18.6121| INFO|Program.Main => Program.SaveOracleToFile => classLog.LogInfo Zapis do katalogu C:\dyskD\wywal\testScan\Stat\statystykaOracle_20210319.csv
2021-04-28 14:46:18.6121| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 14:46:18.6121| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 14:46:18.6170| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-20') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-20') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id

 t.issuccess=1

  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,

2021-04-28 14:46:58.9070| INFO|Program.Main => Program.SaveOracleToFile => classLog.LogInfo Zapis do katalogu C:\dyskD\wywal\testScan\Stat\statystykaOracle_20210330.csv
2021-04-28 14:46:58.9070| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 14:46:58.9070| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 14:46:58.9070| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-03-31') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-03-31') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id

 t.issuccess=1

  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,

LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

2021-04-28 14:48:02.6586| INFO|Program.Main => Program.SaveOracleToFile => classLog.LogInfo Zapis do katalogu C:\dyskD\wywal\testScan\Stat\statystykaOracle_20210410.csv
2021-04-28 14:48:02.6586| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 14:48:02.6586| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 14:48:02.6586| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-04-11') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-04-11') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

2021-04-28 14:49:47.9935| INFO|Program.Main => Program.SaveOracleToFile => classLog.LogInfo Zapis do katalogu C:\dyskD\wywal\testScan\Stat\statystykaOracle_20210421.csv
2021-04-28 14:49:47.9935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo ====================================================================================================
2021-04-28 14:49:47.9935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo Sklepy sprzedaz
2021-04-28 14:49:47.9935| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo with terminalTR as(select k.id KasaId,
sum(
CASE
WHEN (dt.symbol='FVKOR' or dt.symbol='PARKOR') THEN -1*nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)

ELSE nvl2(t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amountinterminalcurrency,t.amount)
END) as Terminal

from POS.nposterminaltransakcja t
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d on t.dokumentid=d.id and  t.issuccess=1
inner join pos.nposdzien dz on d.dzienid=dz.id
inner join POS.nposdokumenttyp dt on d.dokumenttypid=dt.id
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id 
inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-04-22') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-04-22') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

inner join POS.nposkasa k on k.stanowiskoid=st.id
where  (dz.Data='2021-04-27') and
 t.issuccess=1
 group by k.id),
 ksiegowa as (SELECT  
  l.Symbol AS NumerSklep,

  st.Nr as Stanowisko,
  formaPlat.id as formaPlatid,
  sum(tot.Netto) as netto, 
  sum(tot.Brutto) as brutto, 
  sum(tot.Vat) as vat,    
  sum(tot.Ilosc) as ilosc,
 dz.id dzienid,
 kasa.Id kasid 
FROM pos.NSysLokal l
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDzien dz ON dz.LokalID= l.ID
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokument d ON d.DzienID= dz.ID AND d.FlgImportowany= 0
inner join POS.nsysstanowisko st on d.stanowiskoid=st.id
inner join POS.nposkasa kasa on st.id=kasa.stanowiskoid
INNER JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTyp dt ON dt.ID= d.DokumentTypID AND  dt.FlgTyp= 1 AND dt.FlgRodzajSpr= 0 AND dt.FlgKorekta= 0
INNER JOIN pos.NSysOperator oper ON oper.ID= d.OperatorID
inner join POS.nposplatnoscforma formaPlat on formaPlat.flgtyp=1
LEFT JOIN pos.NPosDokumentTotalizer tot ON tot.DokumentID= d.ID

left join pos.nsyskraj kr on l.krajid = kr.id

WHERE

    (kr.symbol = 'PL')  and
   --l.nr=1146 and
   l.opis not like ('Gino%') and
    (dz.Data='2021-04-27') group by   l.Symbol,st.Nr,dz.id,kasa.id,formaPlat.id)select 
    ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko,max(ksiegowa.brutto) Brutto,sum(plat.utarg) Karta,max(
    CASE
WHEN tg.terminal is  NULL THEN 0.0

ELSE tg.terminal
END) Terminal  from ksiegowa
    left join terminalTR tg on ksiegowa.kasid=tg.kasaid
    left join POS.nposzmianatotalizer plat on plat.kasaid=ksiegowa.kasid and plat.dzienid=ksiegowa.dzienid
  and plat.platnoscformaid=ksiegowa.formaPlatid

group by ksiegowa.numersklep,ksiegowa.stanowisko

2021-04-28 14:50:25.6842| INFO|Program.Main => classFun.SoldOracle => classLog.LogInfo SELECT Lokal.symbol NumerSklep,s.Nr Stanowisko,lokal.opis as ShopName
FROM POS.NSYSLOKAL Lokal
join POS.nsysstanowisko s on s.lokalid=Lokal.id
INNER JOIN POS.NSYSKRAJ Kraj on kraj.id = lokal.krajid
WHERE lokal.opis not like ('%Gino%')
and lokal.dataotwarcia <'2021-04-27' and (lokal.datazamkniecia >'2021-04-27' or trunc(lokal.datazamkniecia) = '1900-01-01' )and kraj.symbol ='PL' and lokal.Nr not in(0,4000,199999,1732,3235,2308) and s.nazwa like 'POS%'
order by 1,2
